to_compute_non_colonial_development = {
	set_variable = {
		which = $VARIABLE$
		value = 0
	}
	every_owned_province = {
		limit = {
			is_city = yes
		}
		PREV = {
			export_to_variable = {
				which = to_local_dev
				value = trigger_value:development
				who = PREV
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = $VARIABLE$
				which = to_local_dev
			}
		}
	}
}

to_compute_current_year_in_byzantine_calendar = {
	export_to_variable = {
		which = to_currentYearByzantineCalendar
		value = trigger_value:is_year
	}
	change_variable = {
		which = to_currentYearByzantineCalendar
		value = 5508
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_month = 8
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = to_currentYearByzantineCalendar
			value = 1
		}
	}
}

to_setup_non_hellenic_pagan_provinces = {
	every_province = {
		limit = {
			religion_group = pagan
			NOT = { religion = pantheon_worship }
		}
		set_province_flag = to_non_hellenic_pagan_religion
	}
}

to_check_non_hellenic_pagan_provinces_manual_conversion = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = to_converted_heretics_as_hellenic_potential
		}
		clr_province_flag = to_converted_heretics_as_hellenic_potential
		owner = {
			set_country_flag = to_converted_heretics_as_hellenic
		}
	}
}

to_check_non_hellenic_pagan_provinces = {
	clr_province_flag = to_converted_heretics_as_hellenic_potential
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = to_non_hellenic_pagan_religion
			OR = {
				religion = pantheon_worship
				NOT = { religion_group = pagan }
			}
		}
		clr_province_flag = to_non_hellenic_pagan_religion
		if = {
			limit = {
				religion = pantheon_worship
				owner = {
					religion = pantheon_worship
				}
			}
			set_province_flag = to_converted_heretics_as_hellenic_potential
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_province_flag = to_non_hellenic_pagan_religion }
			religion_group = pagan
			NOT = { religion = pantheon_worship }
		}
		set_province_flag = to_non_hellenic_pagan_religion
	}
}

to_save_years_of_nationalism = {
	hidden_effect = {
		set_variable = {
			which = to_saved_years_of_nationalism
			value = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				nationalism = 1
				NOT = { has_province_flag = to_separatism_restore_pending }
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = to_saved_years_of_nationalism
				value = trigger_value:nationalism
			}
			subtract_variable = {
				which = to_saved_years_of_nationalism
				value = 2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = to_kastrioti_dominion_penalty
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = to_saved_years_of_nationalism
					value = -10
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

to_load_years_of_nationalism = {
	hidden_effect = {
		add_nationalism = -100
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = to_saved_years_of_nationalism
					value = 1
				}
			}
			to_add_correct_exarch_local_nationalism_modifier = yes
		}
	}
}

to_change_tag = {
	to_pre_change_tag_effect = yes
	change_tag = $TAG$
	[[ADDITIONAL_EFFECT]
	$ADDITIONAL_EFFECT$
	]
	on_change_tag_effect = yes
}

to_on_rebels_siege_province_land_share = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				religion = $religion$
				has_estate = estate_church
			}
		}
		owner = {
			change_estate_land_share = {
				estate = estate_church
				share = 10.0
				province = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

to_on_rebels_enforce_demands_land_share = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			religion = $religion$
			has_estate = estate_church
		}
		change_estate_land_share = {
			estate = estate_church
			share = 10.0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_estate_influence_modifier = {
						estate = estate_church
						modifier = EST_VAL_RELIGIOUS_ZEALOTS_TRIUMPH
					}
				}
			}
			add_estate_influence_modifier = {
				estate = estate_church
				desc = EST_VAL_RELIGIOUS_ZEALOTS_TRIUMPH
				duration = 3650
				influence = 15
			}
		}
	}
}

to_replace_idea_group = {
	remove_idea_group = $IDEA_GROUP$
	add_idea_group = $NEW_IDEA_GROUP$
}

to_replace_idea_group_keep_progress = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea_group = $IDEA_GROUP$
			NOT = { has_idea_group = $NEW_IDEA_GROUP$ }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				$IDEA_GROUP$ = 7
			}
			to_replace_idea_group = { IDEA_GROUP = $IDEA_GROUP$ NEW_IDEA_GROUP = $NEW_IDEA_GROUP$ }
			add_idea = $NEW_IDEA_7$
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				$IDEA_GROUP$ = 6
			}
			to_replace_idea_group = { IDEA_GROUP = $IDEA_GROUP$ NEW_IDEA_GROUP = $NEW_IDEA_GROUP$ }
			add_idea = $NEW_IDEA_6$
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				$IDEA_GROUP$ = 5
			}
			to_replace_idea_group = { IDEA_GROUP = $IDEA_GROUP$ NEW_IDEA_GROUP = $NEW_IDEA_GROUP$ }
			add_idea = $NEW_IDEA_5$
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				$IDEA_GROUP$ = 4
			}
			to_replace_idea_group = { IDEA_GROUP = $IDEA_GROUP$ NEW_IDEA_GROUP = $NEW_IDEA_GROUP$ }
			add_idea = $NEW_IDEA_4$
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				$IDEA_GROUP$ = 3
			}
			to_replace_idea_group = { IDEA_GROUP = $IDEA_GROUP$ NEW_IDEA_GROUP = $NEW_IDEA_GROUP$ }
			add_idea = $NEW_IDEA_3$
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				$IDEA_GROUP$ = 2
			}
			to_replace_idea_group = { IDEA_GROUP = $IDEA_GROUP$ NEW_IDEA_GROUP = $NEW_IDEA_GROUP$ }
			add_idea = $NEW_IDEA_2$
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				$IDEA_GROUP$ = 1
			}
			to_replace_idea_group = { IDEA_GROUP = $IDEA_GROUP$ NEW_IDEA_GROUP = $NEW_IDEA_GROUP$ }
			add_idea = $NEW_IDEA_1$
		}
		else = {
			to_replace_idea_group = { IDEA_GROUP = $IDEA_GROUP$ NEW_IDEA_GROUP = $NEW_IDEA_GROUP$ }
		}
	}
}

to_replace_idea_group_with_exploration_keep_progress = {
	to_replace_idea_group_keep_progress = {
		IDEA_GROUP = $IDEA_GROUP$
		NEW_IDEA_GROUP = exploration_ideas
		NEW_IDEA_1 = quest_for_the_new_world
		NEW_IDEA_2 = colonial_ventures
		NEW_IDEA_3 = overseas_exploration
		NEW_IDEA_4 = land_of_opportunity
		NEW_IDEA_5 = vice_roys
		NEW_IDEA_6 = free_colonies
		NEW_IDEA_7 = global_empire
	}
}

to_replace_idea_group_with_exploration_for_ai = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea_group = spy_ideas
		}
		to_replace_idea_group_with_exploration_keep_progress = { IDEA_GROUP = spy_ideas }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea_group = maritime_ideas
		}
		to_replace_idea_group_with_exploration_keep_progress = { IDEA_GROUP = maritime_ideas }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea_group = indigenous_ideas
		}
		to_replace_idea_group_with_exploration_keep_progress = { IDEA_GROUP = indigenous_ideas }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea_group = administrative_ideas
			NOt = { full_idea_group = administrative_ideas }
		}
		to_replace_idea_group_with_exploration_keep_progress = { IDEA_GROUP = administrative_ideas }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea_group = influence_ideas
		}
		to_replace_idea_group_with_exploration_keep_progress = { IDEA_GROUP = influence_ideas }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea_group = diplomatic_ideas
		}
		to_replace_idea_group_with_exploration_keep_progress = { IDEA_GROUP = diplomatic_ideas }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea_group = court_ideas
		}
		to_replace_idea_group_with_exploration_keep_progress = { IDEA_GROUP = court_ideas }
	}
	else_if = {

			has_idea_group = innovativeness_ideas
		}

to_replace_idea_group_with_exploration_master_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_idea_group = exploration_ideas }
			to_there_is_a_switchable_idea_group = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ai = no
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					adm_tech = 5
					NOT = { adm_tech = 7 }
					OR = {
						has_idea_group = spy_ideas
						has_idea_group = maritime_ideas
						has_idea_group = indigenous_ideas
						has_idea_group = administrative_ideas
						has_idea_group = influence_ideas
						has_idea_group = diplomatic_ideas
						has_idea_group = innovativeness_ideas
						has_idea_group = trade_ideas
						has_idea_group = economic_ideas
						has_idea_group = humanist_ideas
						has_idea_group = religious_ideas
						has_idea_group = plutocracy_ideas
						has_idea_group = horde_gov_ideas
						has_idea_group = theocracy_gov_ideas
						has_idea_group = aristocracy_ideas
						has_idea_group = naval_ideas
						has_idea_group = offensive_ideas
						has_idea_group = defensive_ideas
						has_idea_group = quality_ideas
						has_idea_group = quantity_ideas
						has_idea_group = expansion_ideas
						has_idea_group = infrastructure_ideas
						has_idea_group = court_ideas
						has_idea_group = mercenary_ideas
					}
				}
				# Also works for the player if they only have a single idea group
				to_replace_idea_group_with_exploration_for_ai = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						AND = {
							adm_tech = 5
							NOT = { adm_tech = 7 }
							OR = {
								has_idea_group = spy_ideas
								has_idea_group = maritime_ideas
								has_idea_group = indigenous_ideas
								has_idea_group = administrative_ideas
								has_idea_group = influence_ideas
								has_idea_group = diplomatic_ideas
								has_idea_group = innovativeness_ideas
								has_idea_group = trade_ideas
								has_idea_group = economic_ideas
								has_idea_group = humanist_ideas
								has_idea_group = religious_ideas
								has_idea_group = plutocracy_ideas
								has_idea_group = horde_gov_ideas
								has_idea_group = theocracy_gov_ideas
								has_idea_group = aristocracy_ideas
								has_idea_group = naval_ideas
								has_idea_group = offensive_ideas
								has_idea_group = defensive_ideas
								has_idea_group = quality_ideas
								has_idea_group = quantity_ideas
								has_idea_group = expansion_ideas
								has_idea_group = infrastructure_ideas
								has_idea_group = court_ideas
								has_idea_group = mercenary_ideas
							}
						}
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = nhs_new_line_tt
				# custom_tooltip = to_event_to_switch_idea_groups_tt
				country_event = { id = to_colonialism_events.3 tooltip = to_event_to_switch_idea_groups_tt }
			}
		}
		else = {
			to_replace_idea_group_with_exploration_for_ai = yes
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_idea_group = exploration_ideas }
			adm_tech = 5
		}
		add_idea_group = exploration_ideas
	}
}

to_replace_with_next_exarch_idea_group = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_idea_group = humanist_ideas }
		}
		to_replace_idea_group_keep_progress = {
			IDEA_GROUP = $IDEA_GROUP$
			NEW_IDEA_GROUP = humanist_ideas
			NEW_IDEA_1 = local_traditions
			NEW_IDEA_2 = indirect_rule
			NEW_IDEA_3 = ecumenism
			NEW_IDEA_4 = cultural_ties
			NEW_IDEA_5 = humanist_tolerance
			NEW_IDEA_6 = benevolence
			NEW_IDEA_7 = tolerance_idea
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_idea_group = defensive_ideas }
		}

	else_if = {

	else_if = {

			NOT = { has_idea_group = quantity_ideas }
		}
		to_replace_idea_group_keep_progress = {
			IDEA_GROUP = $IDEA_GROUP$
			NEW_IDEA_GROUP = quantity_ideas

to_replace_colonization_ideas_for_exarch = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea_group = exploration_ideas
		}
		to_replace_with_next_exarch_idea_group = {
			IDEA_GROUP = exploration_ideas
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_idea_group = expansion_ideas
		}
		to_replace_with_next_exarch_idea_group = {
			IDEA_GROUP = expansion_ideas
		}
	}
}

to_trigger_colonialism_events_with_portugal = {
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { tag = ROOT }
			to_eligible_for_exploration_event = yes
		}
		country_event = { id = to_colonialism_events.1 }
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				nhs_check_all_elysian_tags = { CONDITION = tag }
			}
			country_event = { id = to_colonialism_events.4 }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				NOT = { nhs_check_all_elysian_tags = { CONDITION = tag } }
				ai = no
				NOT = { to_eligible_for_exploration_event = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					knows_country = ROOT
				}
				country_event = { id = institution_events.300 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = institution_events.301 }
			}
		}
	}
}

to_birthplace_of_colonialism_effect = {
	add_adm_power = 100
	add_dip_power = 100
	add_mil_power = 100
	add_prestige = 20
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_completed_all_reforms_trigger = yes }
		}
		add_reform_progress_medium_effect = yes
	}
	[[ADD_MAGELLAN_EFFECT]
	if =  {
		limit = { 
			has_dlc = "Rights of Man"
			NOT = { num_of_ruler_traits = { amount = 3 } }
			NOT = { ruler_has_personality = navigator_personality }
			has_regency = no
		}
		add_navy_tradition = 10
		add_ruler_personality = navigator_personality
	}
	else = { add_navy_tradition = 20 }
	]
	custom_tooltip = to_colonialism_spread_europe_tt
	custom_tooltip = institution_events.3.a.tt
	custom_tooltip = nhs_new_line_tt
	FROM = {
		add_permanent_province_modifier = {
			name = "birthplace_of_the_new_world"
			duration = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_country_modifier = nhs2_por_ely_trade
				}
			}
			tooltip = {
				add_permanent_province_modifier = {
					name = to_por_gateway_to_elysia
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_province_triggered_modifier = to_por_gateway_to_elysia_tm
			}
		}
	}
	[[ADD_MAGELLAN_EFFECT]
	define_explorer = {
		name = "Ferdinant Magellan"
		shock = 2
		fire = 1
		manuever = 6
		trait = accomplished_sailor_personality
	}
	]
}

to_discover_magellan_travels = {
	custom_tooltip = to_discover_magellan_travels_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		discover_province = 1566

		discover_province = 1581
		discover_province = 1576
		discover_province = 1566
		caribbean_sea_area = {
			discover_country = ROOT
		}
		carribeans_region = {
			limit = {
				has_port = yes
				NOT = { province_id = 481 }
			}
			discover_country = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_saved_event_target = to_magellan_landing

				limit = {

						NOT = { province_id = 481 }
					}
					discover_country = ROOT
				}
			}

						OR = {
							region = mississippi_region

							region = central_america_region

				}

					}
					discover_country = ROOT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {

							OR = {
								region = mexico_region
								region = central_america_region
							}
						}
					}
					every_province = {
						limit = {
							province_group = to_east_coast
							region = event_target:to_magellan_landing
							has_port = yes

						discover_country = ROOT
					}
				}
				else = {
					every_province = {
						limit = {
							region = event_target:to_magellan_landing
							has_port = yes
						}
						discover_country = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:to_magellan_landing = {
						region = colombia_region
					}
				}
				discover_province = 1528
				discover_province = 1527
				# discover_province = 1522
				# discover_province = 1520
				# discover_province = 1519
				# discover_province = 1517
				# discover_province = 1515
				# discover_province = 491
				colombia_region = {
					limit = {
						has_port = yes
					}
					discover_country = ROOT
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:to_magellan_landing = {
						OR = {
							area = north_florida_area
							area = florida_area
							area = south_carolina_area
						}
					}
				}
				bahama_channel_area = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { province_id = 481 }
					}
					discover_country = ROOT
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:to_magellan_landing = {
							OR = {
								area = south_carolina_area
								area = north_florida_area
							}
						}
					}
					discover_province = 1502
				}
				if = {
					limit = {

								area = florida_area

							}

to_accept_magellan_offer = {
	add_dip_power = -100
	custom_tooltip = to_begin_magellan_voyage_tt
	set_global_flag = to_magellan_has_departed
	set_country_flag = to_magellan_departure_country
	save_global_event_target_as = to_magellan_departure_country
	hidden_effect = {
		clear_global_event_target = to_magellan_initial_proposal
		every_country = {
			clr_country_flag = to_denied_magellan
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				nhs_check_all_elysian_tags = { CONDITION = tag }
			}
			country_event = { id = to_colonialism_events.9 days = 90 }
		}
	}
}

to_reject_magellan_offer = {
	add_legitimacy = 10
	hidden_effect = {
		set_country_flag = to_denied_magellan
		set_global_flag = to_magellan_seaches_for_employment
	}
	to_find_new_magellan_target = yes
}

to_find_new_magellan_target = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_country = {
				ai = no
				OR = {
					tag = POR
					tag = CAS
					tag = SPA
				}
				any_owned_province = {
					continent = europe
					sea_zone = {
						region = north_atlantic_region
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						continent = europe
						superregion = africa_superregion
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = to_denied_magellan }
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				ai = no
				OR = {
					tag = POR
					tag = CAS
					tag = SPA
				}
				any_owned_province = {
					continent = europe
					sea_zone = {
						region = north_atlantic_region
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						continent = europe
						superregion = africa_superregion
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = to_denied_magellan }
			}
			country_event = { id = to_colonialism_events.7 days = 30 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_country = {
				ai = no
				religion_group = ROOT
				any_owned_province = {
					continent = europe
					sea_zone = {
						region = north_atlantic_region
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						continent = europe
						superregion = africa_superregion
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = to_denied_magellan }
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				ai = no
				religion_group = ROOT
				any_owned_province = {
					continent = europe
					sea_zone = {
						region = north_atlantic_region
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						continent = europe
						superregion = africa_superregion
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = to_denied_magellan }
			}
			country_event = { id = to_colonialism_events.7 days = 30 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_country = {
				OR = {
					tag = POR
					tag = CAS
					tag = SPA
				}
				any_owned_province = {
					continent = europe
					sea_zone = {
						region = north_atlantic_region
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						continent = europe
						superregion = africa_superregion
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = to_denied_magellan }
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = POR
					tag = CAS
					tag = SPA
				}
				any_owned_province = {
					continent = europe
					sea_zone = {
						region = north_atlantic_region
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						continent = europe
						superregion = africa_superregion
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = to_denied_magellan }
			}
			country_event = { id = to_colonialism_events.7 days = 30 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_country = {
				religion_group = ROOT
				any_owned_province = {
					continent = europe
					sea_zone = {
						region = north_atlantic_region
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						continent = europe
						superregion = africa_superregion
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = to_denied_magellan }
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				religion_group = ROOT
				any_owned_province = {
					continent = europe
					sea_zone = {
						region = north_atlantic_region
					}
				}
				capital_scope = {
					OR = {
						continent = europe
						superregion = africa_superregion
					}
				}
				NOT = { has_country_flag = to_denied_magellan }
			}
			country_event = { id = to_colonialism_events.7 days = 30 }
		}
	}
	else = {
		custom_tooltip = to_magellan_private_financing_tt
		clr_global_flag = to_magellan_seaches_for_employment
		set_global_flag = to_magellan_private_financing
		save_global_event_target_as = to_magellan_private_target
	}
}

to_clean_magellan_flags = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_country = {
			clr_country_flag = to_magellan_departure_country
			clr_country_flag = to_denied_magellan
		}
		every_province = {
			clr_province_flag = to_magellan_landing
		}
		clr_global_flag = to_magellan_has_departed
		clr_global_flag = to_magellan_found_elysia
		clr_global_flag = to_magellan_seaches_for_employment
		clear_global_event_target = to_magellan_departure_country
		clear_global_event_target = to_magellan_initial_proposal
	}
}

to_development_events_add_next_flag = {
	# if = {
	# 	limit = {
	# 		has_province_flag = nhs_had_dev_events_2
	# 	}
	# 	set_province_flag = nhs_had_dev_events_3
	# }
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = nhs_had_dev_events_1
		}
		set_province_flag = nhs_had_dev_events_2
	}
	else = {
		set_province_flag = nhs_had_dev_events_2
	}
}

to_add_2_stability_or_adm_power = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			stability = 3
		}
		add_adm_power = 100
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			stability = 2
		}
		add_stability = 1
		add_adm_power = 50
	}
	else = {
		add_stability = 2
	}
}

to_round_up_variable = {
	change_variable = {
		which = $VARIABLE$
		value = 0.5
	}
	multiply_variable = { 
		which = $VARIABLE$
		value = 0.001
	}
	multiply_variable = { 
		which = $VARIABLE$
		value = 1000
	}
}

to_round_down_variable = {
	multiply_variable = { 
		which = $VARIABLE$
		value = 0.001
	}
	multiply_variable = { 
		which = $VARIABLE$
		value = 1000
	}
}

to_round_down_variable_one_decimal = {
	multiply_variable = { 
		which = $VARIABLE$
		value = 0.01
	}
	multiply_variable = { 
		which = $VARIABLE$
		value = 100
	}
}

to_round_down_variable_two_decimals = {
	multiply_variable = { 
		which = $VARIABLE$
		value = 0.1
	}
	multiply_variable = { 
		which = $VARIABLE$
		value = 10
	}
}

to_remove_var_if_not_0 = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				is_variable_equal = {
					which = $VARIABLE$
					value = 0
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = $VARIABLE$
			value = 0
		}
	}
}


to_remove_historal_friends_and_rivals = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				historical_friend_with = PREV
			}
			remove_historical_friend = PREV
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				PREV = {
					historical_friend_with = PREV
				}
			}
			PREV = {
				remove_historical_friend = PREV
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				historical_rival_with = PREV
			}
			remove_historical_rival = PREV
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				PREV = {
					historical_rival_with = PREV
				}
			}
			PREV = {
				remove_historical_rival = PREV
			}
		}
	}
}

to_save_former_colonial_owner_and_overlord = {
	every_province = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = to_former_colonial_owner@PREV
		}
		clr_province_flag = to_former_colonial_owner@PREV
		set_province_flag = to_former_colonial_owner_TAG
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = to_former_overlord@PREV
		}
		set_country_flag = to_former_overlord_TAG
	}
}

to_load_former_colonial_owner_and_overlord = {
	every_province = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = to_former_colonial_owner_TAG
		}
		clr_province_flag = to_former_colonial_owner_TAG
		set_province_flag = to_former_colonial_owner@PREV
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = to_former_overlord_TAG
		}
		clr_country_flag = to_former_overlord_TAG
		set_country_flag = to_former_overlord@PREV
	}
}

to_save_historal_friends_and_rivals = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				historical_friend_with = PREV
			}
			set_country_flag = to_historical_friend_with_ROOT
			remove_historical_friend = PREV
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				PREV = {
					historical_friend_with = PREV
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = to_ROOT_historical_friend_with_TAG
			PREV = {
				remove_historical_friend = PREV
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				historical_rival_with = PREV
			}
			set_country_flag = to_historical_rival_with_ROOT
			remove_historical_rival = PREV
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				PREV = {
					historical_rival_with = PREV
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = to_ROOT_historical_rival_with_TAG
			PREV = {
				remove_historical_rival = PREV
			}
		}
	}
}

to_load_historal_friends_and_rivals = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = to_historical_friend_with_ROOT
			}
			clr_country_flag = to_historical_friend_with_ROOT
			add_historical_friend = PREV
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = to_ROOT_historical_friend_with_TAG
			}
			clr_country_flag = to_ROOT_historical_friend_with_TAG
			PREV = {
				add_historical_friend = PREV
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = to_historical_rival_with_ROOT
			}
			clr_country_flag = to_historical_rival_with_ROOT
			add_historical_rival = PREV
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = to_ROOT_historical_rival_with_TAG
			}
			clr_country_flag = to_ROOT_historical_rival_with_TAG
			PREV = {
				add_historical_rival = PREV
			}
		}
	}
}

to_restore_historal_friends_and_rivals = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				$PREVIOUS_TAG$ = {
					historical_friend_with = PREV
				}
			}
			$PREVIOUS_TAG$ = {
				remove_historical_friend = PREV
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_historical_friend = PREV
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				$PREVIOUS_TAG$ = {
					PREV = {
						historical_friend_with = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			$PREVIOUS_TAG$ = {
				PREV = {
					remove_historical_friend = PREV
				}
			}
			add_historical_friend = ROOT
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				$PREVIOUS_TAG$ = {
					historical_rival_with = PREV
				}
			}
			$PREVIOUS_TAG$ = {
				remove_historical_rival = PREV
			}
			ROOT = {
				add_historical_rival = PREV
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				$PREVIOUS_TAG$ = {
					PREV = {
						historical_rival_with = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			$PREVIOUS_TAG$ = {
				PREV = {
					remove_historical_rival = PREV
				}
			}
			add_historical_rival = ROOT
		}
	}
}

to_monuments_later = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			$PROVINCE_ID$ = {
				construction_progress = 0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				$PROVINCE_ID$ = {
					has_construction = colonist
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = to_monuments_later_colonist_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				$PROVINCE_ID$ = {
					has_construction = missionary
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = to_monuments_later_missionary_tt
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = to_monuments_later_tt
		}
		custom_tooltip = nhs_new_line_tt
	}
}

to_correct_colony_culture = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_colonial_nation = yes
		}
		overlord = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { nhs_post_fragmentation_culturally_elysian = yes }
				}
				PREV = {
					change_primary_culture = PREV
					set_ruler_culture = PREV
				}
			}
			else = {
				PREV = {
					to_ely_country_culture_check = { 
						FLAG_SCOPE = PREV
						FLAG_SCOPE_BACKUP = yes
					}
				}
			}
			PREV = {
				change_religion = PREV
			}
		}
	}
}

to_subject_monument_mod_transfer = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				is_subject = yes
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = to_subject_monument_mod_transfer_subject_tt
	}
	else = {
		custom_tooltip = to_subject_monument_mod_transfer_tt
	}
}

to_handle_subject_annexation_date = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = to_do_not_change_annexation_date }
		}
		clr_country_flag = to_became_a_subject
		set_country_flag = to_became_a_subject
		export_to_variable = {
			which = to_protectorate_annexation_year_20
			value = trigger_value:is_year
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = to_protectorate_annexation_year_50
			which = to_protectorate_annexation_year_20
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = to_protectorate_annexation_year_20
			value = 20
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = to_protectorate_annexation_year_50
			value = 50
		}
		export_to_variable = {
			which = to_protectorate_annexation_month
			value = trigger_value:is_month
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = to_protectorate_annexation_month
			value = 2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = to_protectorate_annexation_month
					value = 13
				}
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = to_protectorate_annexation_year_20
				value = 1
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = to_protectorate_annexation_year_50
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = to_protectorate_annexation_month
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

to_set_isolation_to_VALUE = {
	custom_tooltip = to_set_isolation_to_$VALUE$_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		set_isolationism = 0
	}
}

nhs_set_center_of_trade_1 = {
	custom_tooltip = nhs_add_center_of_trade_1_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		remove_province_modifier = to_dynamic_cot
		remove_province_triggered_modifier = to_dynamic_cot_tm
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
			}
			center_of_trade = 1
		}
		else = {
			owner = {
				add_treasury = 50
			}
		}
		to_check_trade_center_modifiers_from_privileges = yes
	}
}

nhs_set_center_of_trade_2 = {
	custom_tooltip = nhs_add_center_of_trade_2_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		remove_province_modifier = to_dynamic_cot
		remove_province_triggered_modifier = to_dynamic_cot_tm
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
			}
			center_of_trade = 2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 2 }
			}
			add_center_of_trade_level = 1
		}
		else = {
			owner = {
				add_treasury = 100
			}
		}
		to_check_trade_center_modifiers_from_privileges = yes
	}
}

nhs_set_center_of_trade_3 = {
	custom_tooltip = nhs_add_center_of_trade_3_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		remove_province_modifier = to_dynamic_cot
		remove_province_triggered_modifier = to_dynamic_cot_tm
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
			}
			center_of_trade = 3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 3 }
			}
			add_center_of_trade_level = 2
		}
		else = {
			owner = {
				add_treasury = 500
			}
		}
		to_check_trade_center_modifiers_from_privileges = yes
	}
}

nhs_set_center_in_a_region_to_level_3 = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_owned_province = {
				$CONDITION$
				province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 2
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 3 }
			}
		}
		nhs_set_center_of_trade_3 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_owned_province = {
				$CONDITION$
				province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 3 }
			}
		}
		nhs_set_center_of_trade_3 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_province = {
				$CONDITION$
				country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT
				province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 2
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 3 }
			}
		}
		nhs_set_center_of_trade_3 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_province = {
				$CONDITION$
				country_or_non_sovereign_subject_holds = ROOT
				province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 3 }
			}
		}
		nhs_set_center_of_trade_3 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_province = {
				$CONDITION$
				country_or_subject_holds = ROOT
				province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 2
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 3 }
			}
		}
		nhs_set_center_of_trade_3 = yes
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_province = {
				$CONDITION$
				country_or_subject_holds = ROOT
				province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 3 }
			}
		}
		nhs_set_center_of_trade_3 = yes
	}
	else = {
		add_treasury = 750
	}
}

nhs_set_center_in_a_region = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_owned_province = {
				$TYPE$ = $CNRG$
				province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 2 }
			}
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				$TYPE$ = $CNRG$
				province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 2 }
			}
			nhs_set_center_of_trade_2 = yes
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_owned_province = {
				nhs_eicticofminh = yes
				$TYPE$ = $CNRG$
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
			}
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				nhs_eicticofminh = yes
				$TYPE$ = $CNRG$
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
			}
			nhs_set_center_of_trade_1 = yes
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_province = {
				owner = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				nhs_eicticofminh = yes
				$TYPE$ = $CNRG$
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
			}
		}
		random_province = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				nhs_eicticofminh = yes
				$TYPE$ = $CNRG$
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
			}
			nhs_set_center_of_trade_1 = yes
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			any_province = {
				owner = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				nhs_eicticofminh = yes
				$TYPE$ = $CNRG$
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
			}
		}
		random_province = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				nhs_eicticofminh = yes
				$TYPE$ = $CNRG$
				NOT = { province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1 }
			}
			nhs_set_center_of_trade_1 = yes
		}
	}
	else = {
		add_treasury = 75
	}
}

to_add_government_reform_short_tooltip = {
	custom_tooltip = to_add_$REFORM$_gov_reform_tt
	hidden_effect = {

	}
}

to_non_abrahamic_conversion_penalty_check_province = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			to_has_abrahamic_religion = yes
			owner = {
				NOT = { to_has_abrahamic_religion = yes }
				NOT = { mission_completed = to_the_old_gods_mission }
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						is_subject = yes
						overlord = {
							OR = {
								mission_completed = to_the_old_gods_mission
								AND = {
									is_subject = yes
									overlord = {
										mission_completed = to_the_old_gods_mission
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = to_abrahamic_conversion_penalty
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = to_abrahamic_conversion_penalty
		}
		remove_province_modifier = to_abrahamic_conversion_penalty
	}
}

to_non_abrahamic_conversion_penalty_check_country = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				to_has_abrahamic_religion = yes
				mission_completed = to_the_old_gods_mission
				AND = {
					is_subject = yes
					overlord = {
						OR = {
							mission_completed = to_the_old_gods_mission
							AND = {
								is_subject = yes
								overlord = {
									mission_completed = to_the_old_gods_mission
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = to_abrahamic_conversion_penalty
			}
			remove_province_modifier = to_abrahamic_conversion_penalty
		}
	}
	else = {
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				to_has_abrahamic_religion = yes
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = to_abrahamic_conversion_penalty
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

to_clear_RELIGION_defender_of_faith_et = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_saved_global_event_target = to_$RELIGION$_dof
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					is_defender_of_faith = yes
					religion = $RELIGION$
				}
			}
		}
		clear_global_event_target = to_$RELIGION$_dof
	}
}

to_remove_building_with_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_building = $BUILDING$
		}
		[[VISIBLE_EFFECT]$VISIBLE_EFFECT$]
		hidden_effect = {
			$EFFECT$
			remove_building = $BUILDING$	
		}
	}
}

to_effect_if_building_exists = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_building = $BUILDING$
		}
		$EFFECT$
	}
}

to_building_on_build_effect = {
	to_building_on_build_effect_ely = { BUILDING = $BUILDING$ }
}

to_building_on_build_with_obsolete_effect = {
	to_building_on_build_with_obsolete_effect_ely = {
		BUILDING = $BUILDING$
		OLD_BUILDING = $OLD_BUILDING$
	}
}

to_building_on_build_with_two_obsolete_effect = {

		BUILDING = $BUILDING$
		OLD_BUILDING = $OLD_BUILDING$
		OLD_BUILDING_2 = $OLD_BUILDING_2$
	}
}

		BUILDING = $BUILDING$
		OLD_BUILDING = $OLD_BUILDING$
		OLD_BUILDING_2 = $OLD_BUILDING_2$
		OLD_BUILDING_3 = $OLD_BUILDING_3$
	}
}

to_manufactory_on_build_effect = {
	to_manufactory_on_build_effect_ely = { BUILDING = $BUILDING$ }
}

to_building_on_destroyed = {
	to_building_on_destroyed_effect_ely = {
		BUILDING = $BUILDING$
		[[TIER_1] TIER_1 = yes ]
		[[TIER_2] TIER_2 = yes ]
		[[TIER_3] TIER_3 = yes ]
		[[TIER_4] TIER_4 = yes ]
	}
}

##################################################
# Building counters
##################################################

to_building_counter_clear_flag = {
	clr_province_flag = $FLAG$_$BUILDING$
}
to_building_counter_set_flag = {
	set_province_flag = $FLAG$_$BUILDING$
}
to_building_counter_effect_add = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			[[TRIGGER]
				$TRIGGER$ = yes
			]
			NOT = {
				to_building_counter_had_building = { 
					FLAG = $FLAG$ 
					BUILDING = $BUILDING$ 
				}
			}
		}
		to_building_counter_set_flag = { 
			FLAG = $FLAG$ 
			BUILDING = $BUILDING$ 
		}
		owner = {
			change_variable = {
				which = $VAR$
				value = $VALUE$
			}
			[[COUNT_BUILDING]
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = {
					which = $VAR$_$BUILDING$
					value = 1
				}
			}
			]
		}
		
	}
}
to_building_counter_effect_sub = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			[[TRIGGER]
				$TRIGGER$ = yes
			]
			to_building_counter_had_building = {
				FLAG = $FLAG$ 
				BUILDING = $BUILDING$ 
			}
		}
		to_building_counter_clear_flag = {
			FLAG = $FLAG$ 
			BUILDING = $BUILDING$ 
		}
		owner = {
			subtract_variable = {
				which = $VAR$
				value = $VALUE$
			}
			[[COUNT_BUILDING]
			hidden_effect = {
				subtract_variable = {
					which = $VAR$_$BUILDING$
					value = 1
				}
			}
			]
		}
	}
}
to_building_counter_effect_add_with_obsolete = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			[[TRIGGER]
				$TRIGGER$ = yes
			]
			NOT = {
				to_building_counter_had_building = { 
					FLAG = $FLAG$ 
					BUILDING = $BUILDING$ 
				}
			}
		}
		[[COUNT_BUILDING]
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				change_variable = {
					which = $VAR$_$BUILDING$
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		]
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					to_building_counter_had_building = { 
						FLAG = $FLAG$ 
						BUILDING = $OLD_BUILDING$ 
					}
				}
			}
			to_building_counter_set_flag = { 
				FLAG = $FLAG$ 
				BUILDING = $BUILDING$ 
			}
			owner = {
				change_variable = {
					which = $VAR$ # nhs_HighTierBuildingCount
					value = $VALUE$
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			to_building_counter_clear_flag = { FLAG = $FLAG$ BUILDING = $OLD_BUILDING$ }
			to_building_counter_set_flag = { FLAG = $FLAG$ BUILDING = $BUILDING$ }
			[[OLD_DIF_VALUE]
			owner = {
				change_variable = {
					which = $VAR$ # nhs_HighTierBuildingCount
					value = $OLD_DIF_VALUE$
				}
			}
			]
			[[COUNT_BUILDING]
			hidden_effect = {
				owner = {
					subtract_variable = {
						which = $VAR$_$OLD_BUILDING$
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			]
		}
	}
}
to_building_counter_effect_add_with_two_obsolete = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			[[TRIGGER]
				$TRIGGER$ = yes
			]
			NOT = {
				to_building_counter_had_building = { 
					FLAG = $FLAG$

		[[COUNT_BUILDING]

				}

		}
		]
		if = {
			limit = {
				to_building_counter_had_building = { 
					FLAG = $FLAG$ 
					BUILDING = $OLD_BUILDING$ 
				}
			}
			to_building_counter_clear_flag = { FLAG = $FLAG$ BUILDING = $OLD_BUILDING$ }
			to_building_counter_set_flag = { FLAG = $FLAG$ BUILDING = $BUILDING$ }
			[[OLD_DIF_VALUE]
			owner = {
				change_variable = {
					which = $VAR$ # nhs_HighTierBuildingCount
					value = $OLD_DIF_VALUE$
				}
			}
			]
			[[COUNT_BUILDING]
			hidden_effect = {
				owner = {
					subtract_variable = {

						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			]
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				to_building_counter_had_building = { 
					FLAG = $FLAG$ 
					BUILDING = $OLD_BUILDING_2$ 
				}
			}
			to_building_counter_clear_flag = { FLAG = $FLAG$ BUILDING = $OLD_BUILDING_2$ }
			to_building_counter_set_flag = { FLAG = $FLAG$ BUILDING = $BUILDING$ }
			[[OLD_DIF_VALUE_2]
			owner = {

						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			]
		}
		else = {
			to_building_counter_set_flag = { 
				FLAG = $FLAG$ 
				BUILDING = $BUILDING$ 
			}
			owner = {
				change_variable = {
					which = $VAR$
					value = $VALUE$
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

to_building_counter_local_province_check_building = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_building = $BUILDING$
			NOT = {
				to_building_counter_had_building = { 
					FLAG = $FLAG$
					BUILDING = $BUILDING$
				} 
			}
		}
		to_building_counter_set_flag = {
			FLAG = $FLAG$
			BUILDING = $BUILDING$
		}
		owner = {
			change_variable = {
				which = $VAR$
				value = $VALUE$
			}
			[[COUNT_BUILDING]
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = {
					which = $VAR$_$BUILDING$
					value = 1
				}
			}
			]
		}
	}
}
to_building_counter_local_province_check_manufactory = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_building = $BUILDING$
			NOT = {
				to_building_counter_had_building = { 
					FLAG = $FLAG$
					BUILDING = manufactory
				} 
			}
		}
		to_building_counter_set_flag = {
			FLAG = $FLAG$
			BUILDING = manufactory
		}
		owner = {
			change_variable = {
				which = $VAR$
				value = $VALUE$
			}
			[[COUNT_BUILDING]
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = {
					which = $VAR$_manufactory
					value = 1
				}
			}
			]
		}
	}
}
to_building_counter_former_province_check_building = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			to_building_counter_had_building = { 
				FLAG = $FLAG$
				BUILDING = $BUILDING$
			} 
		}
		to_building_counter_clear_flag = {
			FLAG = $FLAG$
			BUILDING = $BUILDING$  
		}
		FROM = {
			subtract_variable = {
				which = $VAR$
				value = $VALUE$
			}
			[[COUNT_BUILDING]
			hidden_effect = {
				subtract_variable = {
					which = $VAR$_$BUILDING$
					value = 1
				}
			}
			]
		}
	}
}

}

##################################################
# Missionary Strength from battles mechanic
##################################################

to_missionary_strength_from_battles_clear_flags = {
	clr_province_flag = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_cd
	# If you want this to work on other religions add more flags here
	clr_province_flag = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_aztlan
}

to_add_missionary_strength_from_battles = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			unit_owner = {
				has_government_attribute = to_missionary_strength_from_battles
			}
		}
		unit_owner = {
			save_event_target_as = to_battle_won_unit_tar
		}
		location = {
			area = {
				limit = {
					is_empty = no
					NOT = { religion = event_target:to_battle_won_unit_tar }
					owner = {
						OR = {
							tag = event_target:to_battle_won_unit_tar
							war_with = event_target:to_battle_won_unit_tar
						}
					}
					# If you want this to work on other religions expand this
					# OR = {
					# 	NOT = { to_has_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 4 } }
					# 	to_has_missionary_strength_from_battles_incorrect_religion = {
					# 		COUNTRY_SCOPE = event_target:to_battle_won_unit_tar 
					# 	}
					# }
					OR = {
						NOT = { has_province_flag = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_cd }
						had_province_flag = {
							flag = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_cd
							days = 1
						}
					}
				}
				# If you want this to work on other religions expand this
				# if = {
				# 	limit = {
				# 		to_has_missionary_strength_from_battles_incorrect_religion = { 
				# 			COUNTRY_SCOPE = event_target:to_battle_won_unit_tar 
				# 		}
				# 	}
				# 	to_missionary_strength_from_battles_clear_flags = yes
				# 	to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 1 }
				# 	to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 2 }
				# 	to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 3 }
				# 	to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 4 }
				# }

				clr_province_flag = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_cd
				set_province_flag = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_cd
				if = {
					limit = {
						owner = {
							tag = event_target:to_battle_won_unit_tar
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							to_has_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 3 }
						}
						to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 3 }
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_4
							duration = -1
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							to_has_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 2 }
						}
						to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 2 }
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_3
							duration = -1
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							to_has_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 1 }
						}
						to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 1 }
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_2
							duration = -1
						}
					}
					else = {
						add_province_modifier = {
							name = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_1
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					# If you want this to work on other religions expand this
					if = {
						limit = {
							event_target:to_battle_won_unit_tar = {
								religion = aztlan_worship
							}
						}
						set_province_flag = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_aztlan
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							to_has_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 3 }
						}
						to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 3 }
						add_permanent_province_modifier = {
							name = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_inactive_4
							duration = -1
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							to_has_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 2 }
						}
						to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 2 }
						add_permanent_province_modifier = {
							name = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_inactive_3
							duration = -1
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							to_has_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 1 }
						}
						to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 1 }
						add_permanent_province_modifier = {
							name = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_inactive_2
							duration = -1
						}
					}
					else = {
						add_permanent_province_modifier = {
							name = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_inactive_1
							duration = -1
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = {
	remove_province_modifier = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_$TIER$
	remove_province_modifier = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_inactive_$TIER$
}

to_activate_missionary_strength_from_battles = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_inactive_4
		}
		remove_province_modifier = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_inactive_4
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_4
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_inactive_3
		}
		remove_province_modifier = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_inactive_3
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_3
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_inactive_2
		}
		remove_province_modifier = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_inactive_2
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_2
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_modifier = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_inactive_1
		}
		remove_province_modifier = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_inactive_1
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_1
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}

to_check_missionary_strength_from_battles = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			to_has_missionary_strength_from_battles_inactive = yes
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = to_battle_won_unit_tar
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_government_attribute = to_missionary_strength_from_battles
					PREV = {
						to_has_missionary_strength_from_battles_correct_religion = { COUNTRY_SCOPE = PREV }
					}
				}
			}
			to_missionary_strength_from_battles_clear_flags = yes
			to_activate_missionary_strength_from_battles = yes
		}
		else = {
			to_missionary_strength_from_battles_clear_flags = yes
			to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 1 }
			to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 2 }
			to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 3 }
			to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 4 }
		}
	}
}

to_missionary_strength_from_battles_after_war = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			$CHECK_IF$
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_at_war = no
			}
			clr_country_flag = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_is_at_war
		}
		[[CHECK_FROM] 
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_at_war = no
				}
				clr_country_flag = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_is_at_war
			}
		}
		]
		every_province = {
			limit = {
				to_has_missionary_strength_from_battles_inactive = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owned_by = PREV
					ROOT = {
						has_government_attribute = to_missionary_strength_from_battles
					}
					to_has_missionary_strength_from_battles_correct_religion = { COUNTRY_SCOPE = PREV }
				}
				to_activate_missionary_strength_from_battles = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								has_government_attribute = to_missionary_strength_from_battles
								NOT = { religion = PREV }
								PREV = {
									to_has_missionary_strength_from_battles_correct_religion = { COUNTRY_SCOPE = PREV }
								}
							}
						}
						NOT = {
							AND = {
								is_at_war = yes
								any_war_enemy_country = {
									has_government_attribute = to_missionary_strength_from_battles
									NOT = { religion = PREV }
									PREV = {
										to_has_missionary_strength_from_battles_correct_religion = { COUNTRY_SCOPE = PREV }
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				to_missionary_strength_from_battles_clear_flags = yes
				to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 1 }
				to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 2 }
				to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 3 }
				to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_TIER = { TIER = 4 }
			}
		}
	}
}

to_remove_missionary_strength_from_battles_from_owned_provinces = {
	every_owned_province = {
		limit = {
			to_has_missionary_strength_from_battles_active = yes
		}
		remove_province_modifier = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_1
		remove_province_modifier = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_2
		remove_province_modifier = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_3
		remove_province_modifier = to_missionary_strength_from_battles_4
	}
}

to_compute_merc_company_size = {
	export_to_variable = {
		which = to_total_development
		value = total_development
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = $OUTPUT_VARIABLE$
		which = to_total_development
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		which = $OUTPUT_VARIABLE$
		value = $REGIMENTS_PER_DEVELOPMENT$
	}
	to_round_down_variable = { VARIABLE = $OUTPUT_VARIABLE$ }
	if = {
		limit = {
			mil_tech = 16
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = to_merc_size_cap
			value = 30
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			mil_tech = 14
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = to_merc_size_cap
			value = 29
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			mil_tech = 11
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = to_merc_size_cap
			value = 27
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			mil_tech = 9
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = to_merc_size_cap
			value = 25
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			mil_tech = 6
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = to_merc_size_cap
			value = 24
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			mil_tech = 5
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = to_merc_size_cap
			value = 22
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			mil_tech = 2
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = to_merc_size_cap
			value = 20
		}
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = {
			which = to_merc_size_cap
			value = 15
		}
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = to_relative_size_mod
		value = $REGIMENTS_PER_DEVELOPMENT$
	}
	divide_variable = {
		which = to_relative_size_mod
		value = 0.05
	}
	multiply_variable = {
		which = to_merc_size_cap
		which = to_relative_size_mod
	}
	to_round_down_variable = { VARIABLE = to_merc_size_cap }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = $OUTPUT_VARIABLE$
				which = to_merc_size_cap
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = $OUTPUT_VARIABLE$
			which = to_merc_size_cap
		}
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = to_total_development
		which = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = to_merc_size_cap
		which = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = to_relative_size_mod
		which = 0
	}
}

to_change_manpower_by_VARIABLE = {
	set_variable = {
		which = to_manpower_change_counter
		which = $VARIABLE$
	}
	while = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = to_manpower_change_counter
				value = 10000
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = to_manpower_change_counter
			value = 10000
		}
		$SCOPE$ = {
			add_manpower = $SIGN$10
		}
	}
	while = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = to_manpower_change_counter
				value = 1000
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = to_manpower_change_counter
			value = 1000
		}
		$SCOPE$ = {
			add_manpower = $SIGN$1
		}
	}
	while = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = to_manpower_change_counter
				value = 100
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = to_manpower_change_counter
			value = 100
		}
		$SCOPE$ = {
			add_manpower = $SIGN$0.1
		}
	}
	while = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = to_manpower_change_counter
				value = 10
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = to_manpower_change_counter
			value = 10
		}
		$SCOPE$ = {
			add_manpower = $SIGN$0.01
		}
	}
	while = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = to_manpower_change_counter
				value = 1
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = to_manpower_change_counter
			value = 1
		}
		$SCOPE$ = {
			add_manpower = $SIGN$0.001
		}
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = to_manpower_change_counter
		which = 0
	}
}

to_check_culture_after_conversion = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_province_flag = to_check_culture_after_conversion
				AND = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					to_has_promoted_local_culture = { LAKONIAN_DELAYED_CHECK = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		clr_province_flag = to_check_culture_after_conversion
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					OR = {
						to_pre_romaic_greek_primary = yes
						nhs_post_fragmentation_culturally_elysian = yes
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						nhs_post_fragmentation_culturally_elysian = yes
					}
					culture = greek
					continent = north_america
				}
				owner = {
					PREV = {
						change_culture = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_province_flag = to_has_lakonian_culture_potential
						AND = {
							has_province_flag = to_has_lakonian_culture_potential_ping
							NOT = { had_province_flag = { flag = to_has_lakonian_culture_potential_ping days = 1 } }
						}
					}
					to_has_promoted_local_culture_flag = { CULTURE = lakonian }
				}
				change_culture = lakonian
			}
			else = {
				to_ely_province_culture_check = {}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					culture_group = norse_g
				}
			}
			to_nhs_assign_correct_vinlandic_culture = {}
		}
	}
}

to_set_appropriate_elysian_culture = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				nhs_post_fragmentation_culturally_elysian = yes
			}
		}
		to_ely_province_culture_check = {}
	}
}

to_set_country_ruler_heir_consort_culture = {
	change_primary_culture = $CULTURE$
	set_ruler_culture = $CULTURE$
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_heir = yes
		}
		set_heir_culture = $CULTURE$
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_consort = yes
		}
		set_consort_culture = $CULTURE$
	}
}

to_set_ruler_heir_consort_culture_if_primary = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			ruler_culture = $PRIMARY_CULTURE$
		}
		set_ruler_culture = $CULTURE$
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_heir = yes
			heir_culture = $PRIMARY_CULTURE$
		}
		set_heir_culture = $CULTURE$
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_consort = yes
			consort_culture = $PRIMARY_CULTURE$
		}
		set_consort_culture = $CULTURE$
	}
}

to_primary_culture_and_ruler_heir_consort_culture_if_primary = {
	tooltip = {
		change_primary_culture = $CULTURE$
	}
	[[ONLY_SHOW_PRIMARY]
	hidden_effect = {
	]
		to_set_ruler_heir_consort_culture_if_primary = {
			CULTURE = $CULTURE$
			PRIMARY_CULTURE = $PRIMARY_CULTURE$
		}
	[[ONLY_SHOW_PRIMARY]
	}
	]
	hidden_effect = {
		change_primary_culture = $CULTURE$
	}
}

to_remove_fraction_of_aggressive_expansion = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				$COUNTRY_TRIGGER$
			}
			while = {
				limit = {
					has_opinion_modifier = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = aggressive_expansion
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = to_ae_counter
					value = 1
				}
				add_aggressive_expansion = {
					who = ROOT
					value = -1
					apply_calc = no
				}
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				which = to_ae_counter
				value = $FRACTION$
			}
			while = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = to_ae_counter
						value = 1
					}
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = to_ae_counter
					value = -1
				}
				add_aggressive_expansion = {
					who = ROOT
					value = 1
					apply_calc = no
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = to_ae_counter
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

to_destroy_forbidden_colonies = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						colonial_region = colonial_eastern_america
						province_id = 953
					}

												}

										}
									}
								}

					}
				}
			}
		}

			name = nhs2_treaty_of_lantanopolis_colonial_growth_reduction
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}

to_remove_revolution_if_you_cannot_get_it = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_dlc = "Emperor"
			owner = {
				OR = {
					nhs_check_all_elysian_tags = { CONDITION = tag }
					nhs_check_all_spartan = { CONDITION = tag }
					tag = VGD
					is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject
					is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject_varangian
				}
			}
		}
		set_revolution_in_province = no
	}
}

to_remove_revolution_if_you_cannot_get_it_all_provinces = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_dlc = "Emperor"
			OR = {
				nhs_check_all_elysian_tags = { CONDITION = tag }
				nhs_check_all_spartan = { CONDITION = tag }
				tag = VGD
				is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject
				is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject_varangian
			}
		}
		every_province = {
			limit = {
				country_or_subject_holds = PREV
			}
			set_revolution_in_province = no
		}
	}
}

to_remove_bad_personality_adm = {
	trigger_switch = {
		on_trigger = $WHO$_has_personality
		embezzler_personality = { remove_$WHO$_personality = embezzler_personality }
		sinner_personality = { remove_$WHO$_personality = sinner_personality }
		greedy_personality = { remove_$WHO$_personality = greedy_personality }
		obsessive_perfectionist_personality = { remove_$WHO$_personality = obsessive_perfectionist_personality }
	}
}

to_remove_bad_personality_dip = {
	trigger_switch = {
		on_trigger = $WHO$_has_personality
		drunkard_personality = { remove_$WHO$_personality = drunkard_personality }
		babbling_buffoon_personality = { remove_$WHO$_personality = babbling_buffoon_personality }
		cruel_personality = { remove_$WHO$_personality = cruel_personality }
		naive_personality = { remove_$WHO$_personality = naive_personality }
		malevolent_personality = { remove_$WHO$_personality = malevolent_personality }
		loose_lips_personality = { remove_$WHO$_personality = loose_lips_personality }
	}
}

to_remove_bad_personality_mil = {
	trigger_switch = {
		on_trigger = $WHO$_has_personality
		craven_personality = { remove_$WHO$_personality = craven_personality }
	}
}

to_remove_and_save_personality = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			$WHO$_has_personality = $PERSONALITY$
		}
		remove_$WHO$_personality = $PERSONALITY$
		set_country_flag = to_had_$PERSONALITY$
	}
}

to_restore_personality = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = to_had_$PERSONALITY$
		}
		clr_country_flag = to_had_$PERSONALITY$
		add_$WHO$_personality = $PERSONALITY$
	}
}

to_add_ruler_heir_personality_or_modifier = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_dlc = "Rights of Man"
			OR = {
				has_regency = no
				has_consort_regency = yes
			}
			OR = {
				NOT = { num_of_ruler_traits = { amount = 3 } }
				ruler_has_bad_adm_personality = yes
				ruler_has_bad_dip_personality = yes
				ruler_has_bad_mil_personality = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				num_of_ruler_traits = { amount = 3 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ruler_has_bad_adm_personality = yes
				}
				to_remove_bad_personality_adm = { WHO = ruler }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					ruler_has_bad_dip_personality = yes
				}
				to_remove_bad_personality_dip = { WHO = ruler }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					ruler_has_bad_mil_personality = yes
				}
				to_remove_bad_personality_mil = { WHO = ruler }
			}
		}
		# Ensure the added trait is displayed fist
		hidden_effect = {
			to_remove_and_save_personalities = { WHO = ruler }
		}
		add_ruler_personality = $RULER_PERSONALITY$
		hidden_effect = {
			to_restore_personalities = { WHO = ruler }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_regency = no
				has_consort_regency = yes
			}
		}
		add_ruler_modifier = {
			name = $RULER_MODIFIER$
			duration = -1
		}
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			has_dlc = "Rights of Man"
			has_heir = yes
			has_regency = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					heir_has_good_adm_personality = yes
					heir_has_good_dip_personality = yes
					heir_has_good_mil_personality = yes
					heir_has_bad_adm_personality = yes
					heir_has_bad_dip_personality = yes
					heir_has_bad_mil_personality = yes
				}
			}
			set_heir_flag = $HEIR_FLAG$
			custom_tooltip = $HEIR_TOOLTIP_PERSONALITY$
		}
		else = {
			add_heir_personality = $HEIR_PERSONALITY$
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_heir = yes
			has_regency = yes
		}
		set_heir_flag = $HEIR_FLAG$
		custom_tooltip = $HEIR_TOOLTIP_MODIFIER$
	}
}

to_check_trade_center_modifiers_from_privileges = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_development_of_cities
			}
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = estate_burghers_development_of_cities_mod }
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = estate_burghers_development_of_cities_mod
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				has_estate_privilege = estate_vaisyas_development_of_cities
			}
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = estate_vaisyas_development_of_cities_mod }
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = estate_vaisyas_development_of_cities_mod
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				has_estate_privilege = estate_jains_development_of_cities
			}
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = estate_jains_development_of_cities_mod }
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = estate_jains_development_of_cities_mod
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	owner = {
		save_event_target_as = to_province_owner
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				has_estate_privilege = estate_burghers_exclusive_trade_rights
			}
			calc_true_if = {
				amount = 3
				all_trade_node_member_province = {
					owned_by = event_target:to_province_owner
					province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
				}
			}
		}
		every_trade_node_member_province = {
			limit = {
				owned_by = event_target:to_province_owner
				province_has_center_of_trade_of_level = 1
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = estate_burghers_exclusive_trade_rights_mod
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
	to_handle_mercantile_nation_cot_boost_modifier = yes
}

to_native_undiscover_provinces_outside_of_capital_region_if_annexed = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { technology_group = FROM }
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					technology_group = north_american
					technology_group = south_american
					technology_group = mesoamerican
					technology_group = andean
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			capital_scope = {
				save_event_target_as = to_annexed_capital_scope
			}
			every_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { region = event_target:to_annexed_capital_scope }
				}
				undiscover_country = PREV
			}
		}
	}
}

to_transfer_colonial_nation = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_subject_of_type = crown_colony
		}
		$OVERLORD_SCOPE$ = {
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = crown_colony
				subject = $COLONY_SCOPE$
				keep_liberty_desire = yes
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			is_subject_of_type = private_enterprise
		}
		$OVERLORD_SCOPE$ = {
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = private_enterprise
				subject = $COLONY_SCOPE$
				keep_liberty_desire = yes
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			is_subject_of_type = self_governing_colony
		}
		$OVERLORD_SCOPE$ = {
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = self_governing_colony
				subject = $COLONY_SCOPE$
				keep_liberty_desire = yes
			}
		}
	}
	else = {
		$OVERLORD_SCOPE$ = {
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = colony
				subject = $COLONY_SCOPE$
				keep_liberty_desire = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

to_handle_subject_colonial_nations_on_becoming_dependancy = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { is_subject_of_type = tributary_state }
			colony = 1
		}
		save_event_target_as = to_overlord
		overlord = {
			save_event_target_as = to_overlord_overlord
		}
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				is_colonial_nation = yes
			}
			# set_country_flag = to_has_former_overlord
			set_country_flag = to_former_overlord@FROM
			every_owned_province = {
				set_province_flag = to_former_colonial_owner@FROM
			}
			to_transfer_colonial_nation = {
				OVERLORD_SCOPE = event_target:to_overlord_overlord
				COLONY_SCOPE = PREV
			}
			country_event = { id = nhs2_test.6 }
		}
	}
}

to_handle_subject_colonial_nations_on_losing_dependancy = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			exists = yes
			ROOT = {
				colony = 1
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = {
					is_colonial_nation = yes
					has_country_flag = to_former_overlord@FROM
				}
				clr_country_flag = to_former_overlord@FROM
				to_transfer_colonial_nation = {
					OVERLORD_SCOPE = FROM
					COLONY_SCOPE = PREV
				}
				every_owned_province = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { has_province_flag = to_former_colonial_owner@FROM }
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_state_core = PREV
							}
							add_core = ROOT
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = {
								is_territorial_core = PREV
							}
							add_territorial_core = ROOT
						}
						cede_province = ROOT
					}
					clr_province_flag = to_former_colonial_owner@FROM
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

to_handle_subject_gaining_colonial_nation = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_colonial_nation = yes
			overlord = {
				is_subject = yes
			}
		}
		save_event_target_as = to_colony
		overlord = {
			save_event_target_as = to_overlord
			overlord = {
				save_event_target_as = to_overlord_overlord
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = to_former_overlord@event_target:to_overlord
		every_owned_province = {
			set_province_flag = to_former_colonial_owner@event_target:to_overlord
		}
		to_transfer_colonial_nation = {
			OVERLORD_SCOPE = event_target:to_overlord_overlord
			COLONY_SCOPE = PREV
		}
		country_event = { id = nhs2_test.6 }
	}
}

to_check_province_transfer_to_overlord_colony = {
	owner = {
		save_event_target_as = to_owner
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_city = yes
			is_empty = no
			is_colony = no
			is_overseas = yes
			to_in_colonial_region = yes
			NOT = { has_province_flag = nhs_is_colony }
			owner = {
				is_subject = yes
				NOT = { has_country_flag = no_colonial_nations }
				NOT = {
					capital_scope = {
						to_in_colonial_region = yes
					}
				}
				overlord = {
					any_subject_country = {
						has_country_flag = to_former_overlord@event_target:to_owner
						capital_scope = {
							colonial_region = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			overlord = {
				random_subject_country = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = to_former_overlord@event_target:to_owner
						capital_scope = {
							colonial_region = ROOT
						}
					}
					ROOT = {
						cede_province = PREV
						set_province_flag = to_former_colonial_owner@event_target:to_owner
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

to_remove_former_colonial_owner = {
	every_province = {
		clr_province_flag = to_former_colonial_owner@PREV
	}
	every_country = {
		clr_country_flag = to_former_overlord@PREV
	}
}

to_save_great_project_levels = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_great_project = { type = nhs_cothon tier = 0 } }
		if = {
			limit = { has_great_project = { type = nhs_cothon tier = 3 } }
			set_province_flag = to_had_great_project_nhs_cothon_tier_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_great_project = { type = nhs_cothon tier = 2 } }
			set_province_flag = to_had_great_project_nhs_cothon_tier_2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_great_project = { type = nhs_cothon tier = 1 } }
			set_province_flag = to_had_great_project_nhs_cothon_tier_1
		}
		else = {
			set_province_flag = to_had_great_project_nhs_cothon_tier_0
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_great_project = { type = nhs_alexandrian_library tier = 0 } }
		if = {
			limit = { has_great_project = { type = nhs_alexandrian_library tier = 3 } }
			set_province_flag = to_had_great_project_nhs_alexandrian_library_tier_3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_great_project = { type = nhs_alexandrian_library tier = 2 } }
			set_province_flag = to_had_great_project_nhs_alexandrian_library_tier_2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_great_project = { type = nhs_alexandrian_library tier = 1 } }

					has_great_project = { type = suez_canal tier = 3 }
				}
				add_great_project_tier = { type = suez_canal tier = -3 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_great_project = { type = suez_canal tier = 2 }
					NOT = { has_great_project = { type = suez_canal tier = 3 } }
				}
				add_great_project_tier = { type = suez_canal tier = -2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_great_project = { type = suez_canal tier = 1 }
					NOT = { has_great_project = { type = suez_canal tier = 2 } }
				}
				add_great_project_tier = { type = suez_canal tier = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 0 } }
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = to_had_great_project_panama_canal_tier_3 }
			clr_province_flag = to_had_great_project_panama_canal_tier_3
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 2 }
					NOT = { has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 3 } }
				}
				add_great_project_tier = { type = panama_canal tier = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 1 }
					NOT = { has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 2 } }
				}
				add_great_project_tier = { type = panama_canal tier = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 0 }
					NOT = { has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 1 } }
				}
				add_great_project_tier = { type = panama_canal tier = 3 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = to_had_great_project_panama_canal_tier_2 }
			clr_province_flag = to_had_great_project_panama_canal_tier_2
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 3 }
				}
				add_great_project_tier = { type = panama_canal tier = -1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 1 }
					NOT = { has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 2 } }
				}
				add_great_project_tier = { type = panama_canal tier = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 0 }
					NOT = { has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 1 } }
				}
				add_great_project_tier = { type = panama_canal tier = 2 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = to_had_great_project_panama_canal_tier_1 }
			clr_province_flag = to_had_great_project_panama_canal_tier_1
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 3 }
				}
				add_great_project_tier = { type = panama_canal tier = -2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 2 }
					NOT = { has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 3 } }
				}
				add_great_project_tier = { type = panama_canal tier = -1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 0 }
					NOT = { has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 1 } }
				}
				add_great_project_tier = { type = panama_canal tier = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_province_flag = to_had_great_project_panama_canal_tier_0 }
			clr_province_flag = to_had_great_project_panama_canal_tier_0
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 3 }
				}
				add_great_project_tier = { type = panama_canal tier = -3 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 2 }
					NOT = { has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 3 } }
				}
				add_great_project_tier = { type = panama_canal tier = -2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 1 }
					NOT = { has_great_project = { type = panama_canal tier = 2 } }
				}
				add_great_project_tier = { type = panama_canal tier = -1 }
			}
		}
	}
}
